                    <script type="text/javascript">
                        document.getElementById('Header').style.height='407px';
                        function toggleMenu(el1, el2, over) {
                            var p, prefix = 'nav-';
                            if (el2 == -1) p = document.getElementById(prefix + el1);
                            else p = document.getElementById(prefix + el1 + '-' + el2);
                            if (over == 1) { var newClassName = p.className + " over"; p.className = newClassName; }
                            else { var newClassName = p.className.replace(" over", ""); p.className = newClassName; }
                        }
                    </script>

    function changeMFA(id, mfa_id,mfa_count) {
        document.getElementById('mfaid').value=mfa_id;
        view_facturer('0');
        document.getElementById(id+'_img').innerHTML='<img onmouseover="obj_filter(this,80);" onmouseout="obj_filter(this,100);" style="cursor:pointer;margin-left:5px;" title="Huỷ lọc theo hãng" src="http://daikin.info.vn/talawebstatic/images/icon/delete_f2.png" border="0" width="14" alt=""/>';

            if(id!='mfa_li_'+i) {
                document.getElementById('mfa_li_'+i).style.display='none';
            }
        }
    }

        document.getElementById('mfaid').value="";

            document.getElementById('mfa_li_'+i).style.display='';
            document.getElementById('mfa_li_'+i+'_img').innerHTML='';

        view_facturer('0');
    }

        reloadMFA(mfa_count);

            function SetViewTableDiv(tableName)
            {
                var str = AdFindObjectID(tableName + 'Loc').style.display;
                if (str == 'block')
                {
                    AdFindObjectID(tableName + 'Loc').style.display = "none";
                    AdFindObjectID(tableName).src = "http://daikin.info.vn/skins/pink/images/AdImgDown.gif";
                }
                else
                {
                    AdFindObjectID(tableName + 'Loc').style.display = "block";
                    AdFindObjectID(tableName).src = "http://daikin.info.vn/skins/pink/images/AdImgUp0.gif";
                }
    
            }

            function update_weight(v)
            {
                var w='0-50';
                if(v<=50)
                    w='0-50';
                else if(v<=100)
                    w='50-100';
                else if(v<=250)
                    w='100-250';
                else if(v<=500)
                    w='250-500';
                else if(v<=1000)
                    w='500-1000';
                else if(v<=500)
                    w='1000-1500';
                else if(v<=2000)
                    w='1500-2000';
                else if(v>2000)
                    w='>2000';
                document.getElementById('weightid').value=w;

            }

                cur_cat=i;
